 The month of Sawan has great significance in Hinduism
 aaj se sawan ke pavitra maheene kii shuruuaat ho gai he
 This holy month will start from July 17 and will continue till August 15
 bhagwaan shiv ko samarpit is maheene ko sabase pavitra maheenaa mana jaataa he
 According to Hinduism, this month is very dear to Lord Shiva
 aaie jaanate hai sawan main kaise kerani chahie bhole kii puja or kya he shivaratri kii puja vidhi or shubh muhoort
 The first Monday of Sawan will be on 22 July this time
 iske baad doosraa somvaar 29, teesraa 5 agast or chauthaa 12 agast ko padegaa

 jo ki guuruuvaar kaa din hoga
 When is Shivaratri of Sawan - Shivaratri of Sawan is said to have special significance in Hinduism
 manyataon ke anusaar shivaratri ke din bhagwaan shiv par jal chadhaane se bholenath prasann hokar manokamana puri karte hai
 This time Shivaratri of Sawan is falling on 30th July
 us din mangalvaar kaa din he
 On this day, people offer bell leaf and datura on the Shivling
 shivaratri ke din puja kaa shubh muhoort-sawan kii shivaratri par puja kaa shubh muhoort subah 9
 It will be from 10 to 2 pm
 haalanki jyotishiyon kii maane to shivaratri kaa puraa din hi puja ke liye behad shubh rahata he
 Devotees can worship Lord Shiva on this day at any time
 har saal padati hai 12 shivaratri-bhagwaan shiv ke bhakton ke liye har saal 12 shivaratriyaan aati hai jo ki har trayodashi ke din padati hai
 On the day of Shivratri, people fast and offer prayers to Lord Shankar
 manyata he ki agar koi kunvaari kanya shivaratri kaa vrath rakhti he to use manachaaha var miltaa he
 Shivaratri falling in Phalgun is worshiped as Mahashivratri
 mana jaataa he ki isi din shiv parvati kaa vivaah hua tha
 How to do Lord Shiva on Shivaratri: Abhishek - Get up early in the morning on Shivaratri and take a bath
 mandir main jate samay jal, doodh, dahi, shahad, ghi, chini, itr, chandan, kesar, bhaang sabhi ko milkaar ek bartan main saath le jaaen or shivlinga kaa abhishek karen
 Offer these things to Lord Shiva - You can please them quickly by offering things made of wheat to Shiva - It is believed that mung should be offered to Shiva in order to attain the glory
 -shiv ko til chadhaane se paapon kaa naash hota he
 Seventy-one years after independence, today when we are again discussing what freedom and autonomy means to us both in terms of principles and practice, it is probably necessary to remind ourselves of the fact that rights and responsibilities are simultaneously Let's go
 is roshni main ham dekhnaa chahenge ki doctor-marij ke rishte main un adhikaron or jimmedaariyaan ke khaake kaise dikhaai dete hai
 Mutual practice between these two means more than doctor and client
 isse us zyada bade samaaj or kanoonee prabhaavon kii bhi jhalak milti he jo unke aapasi kaamkaaj par bhi anivaary taur par asar daalenge hi
 Therefore, the feeling of autonomy in the mind of the patient at the time of meeting in the clinic will be determined by how society sees the doctor
 isi tarah doctor ke dimag main jo fori ahmiyat kaa ehsaas he, chaahe vah saajha ho yaa ekatarfa, vah bhi kanoon samet kai chizon se prabhavit hota he
 Modern society probably oscillates between two things
 ek taraf vah chikitsa ke peshey ko tamaam aklmandi or paravaahdari kaa akshayakund maanata he or ummid karata he ki vah use road rej se lekar global varming tak tamaam chijen samajhaayega or hameshaa niswaarth nishtha or samarpan ke saath kaam karata rahegaa
 On the other hand, he also sees the medical profession as a tool to make money and snoop, taking advantage of both disease and suffering
 badale main chikitsa kaa pesha bhi behad alag-alag rukhon ke bich buree tarah jhulata najar aata he
 At one level, there is an inherited philanthropic, humanist stance, in which the doctor sees himself as a duty bound to care for and support all the needy, especially the poor and the poor, while at another level there is the temptation of wealth 
 hakeekat yah he ki hindustan main zyaadaatar medical dekhbhaal asal main nijee kshetra main hoti he or vah chikitsa beemaa yaa niyokta ke paise se tay beemaa swasthya seva kaa vaaki bahut chota-sa hissaa hi he
 So most of the healthcare costs ultimately have to be incurred "out of pocket" costs
 is dekhbhaal kaa rangamanch mukhya rup se desh bhar main faile clinics, nursing home or bade tathaa chote aspataal hai
 The second part of this is that effective rules and regulations for medical practice are truly missing
 chikitsa kii mukchay niamak sanstha bhartiya chikitsa parishad (emsiai) ne mushkil se hi koi tarif ke laayak kaam kiya he
 The medical professional association, unlike the UK, is neither in a regulatory role nor is it a licensing officer
 to britain kaa manochikitsak royal college of cycetry kaa licensadhari hota he, magar hindustan main indian cycetry sosayadi manochikitsak ko license nahin detii, emsiai detii he
 Therefore, professional organizations can make recommendations, make practice guidelines, and this is really their job as well, but their job is also to worry about the interests of the members
 yah lakshya, yani practice kar rahe doctoron kaa hit or doctor jis samaaj kaa ilaaj karte hai uskaa hit, beshak hameshaa ek rahane vaala to nahin he
 So while connecting these two is certainly the most important thing, the question is how effectively it happens
 yah bhi yaad rakhana jaruri he ki desh main specialist ke taur par practice karne ke liye doctor ko peshewar sanghon ke saath register hone kii darkaar nahin he
 MCI registration is enough
 is paridrishy main practice ke niyam-kaayade aksar practice kar rahe doctor par hi chhod die jate hai
 The truth is that medical practice is undeniably generally good
 doctoron kii badi taadaad bilashak marij kii bhalaai ko dimag main rakhkar hi kaam karegi or vah marij jo apni sehat or apana bharosa doctor kii dekhbhaal main soup detaa he
 It has become so clear that sometimes this trust will prove to be wrong
 anaavashyak jaanch ke farmaan die jaaenge, gairajaruri prakriyaayein likhi jaaengi, cat-practice yani jaanch or refral main kamishankhori hogi
 Some prescriptions will be illogical
 medical peshey kii dhanalolupata kii inhen misaalon ne bhalmansahat se kii ja rahi practice ke zyada bade hisse ko ek lihaaj se mushkiljada raushnee main dhakel diya he
 The increasing concerns about medical malpractice, as well as the way courts and society are adopting a critical attitude towards medical practice, may also point to this
 inase badhate nirashaavadi ahsaas kii bhi jhalak milti he
 This is indicative of the increasing level of quarreling of society in one sense and on the other it is the understanding that the way any profession should bind itself to the rules may not be visible
 aaj jab hamane kai charchaaen kii hai ki aazaadee or swaittata ke kya myne hai, is baat par vichaar karnaa bhi acha ho saktaa he ki chikitsa samudaay kis kism kii charchaa or bahason par nirbhar he
 The importance of this discussion increases even more in the discipline of psychiatry because it is the discipline in which the constructions of society are influential
 maansik swasthya kanoon khaas taur par isaki ek misaal he
 There is a need to consider the possibility that some people may, at some time - because of their mental disorder - require "involuntary" or "supported" treatment for a short or long time
 yah niyam or anichhaa se ilaaj karavaate vakt vyakti ke adhikaron kii hifaazat maansik swasthya kanoon kaa marm hai
 Also, when it will decide who needs it, who will decide it — doctor, family, court, or committee — these limitations are issues that all societies have to deal with
 ek or udhaaharan vah behad lubhaavni avadharana he jise manochikitsa main "agrim nirdesh'' kaha jaataa he
 In this, the person in the condition of conciliation and health decides what has been done and cannot be done to him in the event of possible future inefficiency
 to iskaa arth yah hua ki main kah rahaa hum ki agar main kisi maansik rog se biimaar pad jaaun to main tay karata hum ki meraa ilaaj kis tarah hoga
 However, in actual practice this raises many interesting and intriguing questions — which self is the decision-making self, how one self can decide for the other, when it can be canceled, and the fact that when we The person transforms into a scandal agreement between doctor and law; There is still a discussion on what happens then

 sheet ritu- uttar bharat ke maidani bhaagon main sheet ritu main varsha pashchim vikshobh yaa jet stream ke kaaran hoti he
 - During the winter (january-february), the monsoon or north eastern monsoon is caused by the returning rain on the shores of Tamil Nadu

 Political history of Basirhat seat When the first general election was held in the country in 1952, this seat was a two-member Lok Sabha constituency
 1952 ke aam chunaavon main yahaan se makapa ke tikat par renu chakravarti ne jeet hasil kii thi
 After him, Congress icon Roy became a Member of Parliament
 1957 ke aam chunaavon main makapa kii renu chakravarti dobaaraa jeet hasil karne main kaamyaab raheen
 Pareshnath Kayal of Congress became MP after him
 1962 ke chunaavon main congress ke ummidavaar humanyu kabir jitkar sansad pahunche
 The Bengali Congress won this seat in the 1967 general elections and Humanyu Kabir became an MP
 1970 ke chunaavon main bangla congress ne dobaaraa is seat par jeet darj kii or sardaar amjad ali loksabhaa chunaav jitkar sansad pahunche
 At the same time, in the general elections held in 1971, AKM Ishq of Congress won while Alhaz M
 of Bharatiya Lok Dal in 1977 elections
 e
 Hannan won
 yah apatkaal ke baad kaa daur jisamen bhartiya lokdal ne pashchim bengal kii kai loksabhaa siton par jeet darj kii thi
 In the 1980 and 1984 elections, Indrajeet Gupta of CPI-M continued to elect and reach Parliament
 1989 or 1991 ke chunaavon main makapa ke manoranjan sur lagaataar chune jate rahe
 CPI candidate Ajay Chakraborty continued to win elections in the 1996, 1998, 1999 and 2004 general elections
 lekin 2009 ke chunaavon main trinmul congress ne pehali baar is seat par jeet darj kii or uske ummidavaar haji nurul islam saansad bane jabaki 2014 ke chunaavon main trinmul ke idris ali chunaav jeetne main safal rahe
